    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [p].[Id], [p].[AzureUniqueId], [p].[Organization], [p].[Role], [p].[Progression], [a].[IsVoided], [q].[Id], [e].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Text], [t].[CreateDate], [t].[c], [t].[Id0], [t].[AzureUniqueId], [t].[Organization], [t].[Role], [t].[Progression], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Text], [t0].[CreateDate], [t0].[c], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[AzureUniqueId], [t0].[Organization], [t0].[Role], [t0].[Progression], CAST(1 AS bit), [q].[Text], [q].[SupportNotes], [q].[Barrier], [q].[Order], [q].[Organization], CAST(1 AS bit), [e].[Name], [p3].[Id], [p3].[AzureUniqueId], [p3].[Organization], [p3].[Role], [p3].[Progression], CAST(1 AS bit), [p0].[FusionProjectId]
FROM [Actions] AS [a]
LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p] ON [a].[AssignedToId] = [p].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Questions] AS [q] ON [a].[QuestionId] = [q].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Evaluations] AS [e] ON [q].[EvaluationId] = [e].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Projects] AS [p0] ON [e].[ProjectId] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [n].[Id], [n].[Text], [n].[CreateDate], CASE
        WHEN [p1].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)

) AS [t] ON [a].[Id] = [t].[ActionId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Text], [c].[CreateDate], CASE
        WHEN [p2].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

) AS [t0] ON [a].[Id] = [t0].[ActionId]
LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p3] ON [e].[Id] = [p3].[EvaluationId]
WHERE [p].[AzureUniqueId] = @__p_0

""SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[Name], [e].[Progression], [e].[CreateDate], [e].[Status], [e].[ProjectId], [e].[IndicatorActivityDate], CAST(1 AS bit), [p].[FusionProjectId], [p].[IndicatorEvaluationId], [p].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Barrier], [t].[Id0], [t].[Severity], [t].[Progression], [t].[Id1], [t].[DueDate], [t].[Completed], [t].[IsVoided]
FROM [Evaluations] AS [e]
INNER JOIN [Projects] AS [p] ON [e].[ProjectId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [q].[Id], [q].[Barrier], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[Severity], [a].[Progression], [a0].[Id] AS [Id1], [a0].[DueDate], [a0].[Completed], [a0].[IsVoided], [q].[EvaluationId]
    FROM [Questions] AS [q]
    LEFT JOIN [Answers] AS [a] ON [q].[Id] = [a].[QuestionId]
    LEFT JOIN [Actions] AS [a0] ON [q].[Id] = [a0].[QuestionId]
) AS [t] ON [e].[Id] = [t].[EvaluationId]
WHERE [e].[Status] = @__p_0
ORDER BY [e].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]"
[11:49:47 Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command [Information] Executed DbCommand ("49"ms) [Parameters=["@__p_0='?' (Size = 450)"], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']"
""SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[Title], [a].[OnHold], [a].[DueDate], [a].[Priority], [a].[Completed], [a].[CreateDate], [a].[Description], CASE
    WHEN [p].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [p].[Id], [p].[AzureUniqueId], [p].[Organization], [p].[Role], [p].[Progression], [a].[IsVoided], [q].[Id], [e].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Text], [t].[CreateDate], [t].[c], [t].[Id0], [t].[AzureUniqueId], [t].[Organization], [t].[Role], [t].[Progression], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Text], [t0].[CreateDate], [t0].[c], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[AzureUniqueId], [t0].[Organization], [t0].[Role], [t0].[Progression], CAST(1 AS bit), [q].[Text], [q].[SupportNotes], [q].[Barrier], [q].[Order], [q].[Organization], CAST(1 AS bit), [e].[Name], [p3].[Id], [p3].[AzureUniqueId], [p3].[Organization], [p3].[Role], [p3].[Progression], CAST(1 AS bit), [p0].[FusionProjectId]
FROM [Actions] AS [a]
LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p] ON [a].[AssignedToId] = [p].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Questions] AS [q] ON [a].[QuestionId] = [q].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Evaluations] AS [e] ON [q].[EvaluationId] = [e].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Projects] AS [p0] ON [e].[ProjectId] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [n].[Id], [n].[Text], [n].[CreateDate], CASE
        WHEN [p1].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c], [p1].[Id] AS [Id0], [p1].[AzureUniqueId], [p1].[Organization], [p1].[Role], [p1].[Progression], [n].[ActionId]
    FROM [Notes] AS [n]
    LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p1] ON [n].[CreatedById] = [p1].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [a].[Id] = [t].[ActionId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Text], [c].[CreateDate], CASE
        WHEN [p2].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c], [p2].[Id] AS [Id0], [p2].[AzureUniqueId], [p2].[Organization], [p2].[Role], [p2].[Progression], [c].[ActionId]

""SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[Title], [a].[OnHold], [a].[DueDate], [a].[Priority], [a].[Completed], [a].[CreateDate], [a].[Description], CASE
    WHEN [p].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [p].[Id], [p].[AzureUniqueId], [p].[Organization], [p].[Role], [p].[Progression], [a].[IsVoided], [q].[Id], [e].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Text], [t].[CreateDate], [t].[c], [t].[Id0], [t].[AzureUniqueId], [t].[Organization], [t].[Role], [t].[Progression], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Text], [t0].[CreateDate], [t0].[c], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[AzureUniqueId], [t0].[Organization], [t0].[Role], [t0].[Progression], CAST(1 AS bit), [q].[Text], [q].[SupportNotes], [q].[Barrier], [q].[Order], [q].[Organization], CAST(1 AS bit), [e].[Name], [p3].[Id], [p3].[AzureUniqueId], [p3].[Organization], [p3].[Role], [p3].[Progression], CAST(1 AS bit), [p0].[FusionProjectId]
FROM [Actions] AS [a]
LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p] ON [a].[AssignedToId] = [p].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Questions] AS [q] ON [a].[QuestionId] = [q].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Evaluations] AS [e] ON [q].[EvaluationId] = [e].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Projects] AS [p0] ON [e].[ProjectId] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [n].[Id], [n].[Text], [n].[CreateDate], CASE
        WHEN [p1].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c], [p1].[Id] AS [Id0], [p1].[AzureUniqueId], [p1].[Organization], [p1].[Role], [p1].[Progression], [n].[ActionId]
    FROM [Notes] AS [n]
    LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p1] ON [n].[CreatedById] = [p1].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [a].[Id] = [t].[ActionId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Text], [c].[CreateDate], CASE
        WHEN [p2].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c], [p2].[Id] AS [Id0], [p2].[AzureUniqueId], [p2].[Organization], [p2].[Role], [p2].[Progression], [c].[ActionId]
    FROM [ClosingRemarks] AS [c]
    LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p2] ON [c].[CreatedById] = [p2].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [a].[Id] = [t0].[ActionId]
LEFT JOIN [Participants] AS [p3] ON [e].[Id] = [p3].[EvaluationId]
WHERE [p].[AzureUniqueId] = @__p_0
ORDER BY [a].[Id], [p].[Id], [q].[Id], [e].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]"

    END AS [c], [p1].[Id] AS [Id0], [p1].[AzureUniqueId], [p1].[Organization], [p1].[Role], [p1].[Progression], [n].[ActionId]
    FROM [Notes] AS [n]

) AS [t] ON [a].[Id] = [t].[ActionId]

    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Text], [c].[CreateDate], CASE
        WHEN [p2].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

) AS [t0] ON [a].[Id] = [t0].[ActionId]

WHERE [p].[AzureUniqueId] = @__p_0
